2a1(mdo): po gadzin cho kyis dben pa'i nganan sakyi ngo bo kun tu 'od kyi 'ang bzangs rgyas po rnams kyi brgyan gyi tshogs rje

2b1(mdo): kyi dmyigs pa la mkhas pa dang ldan pa sha stag go// thams cad kyang rab 'byung gi ye shes kyi sa las ma bskyod pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i lus dang ldan pa sha stag go// thams cad kya
2b2(mdo): thams cad mkhyend pa nyid kyis thob par spyod pa las phyir myi ldog pa sha stag go// thams cad kyang byang chub sems dpa'i mngon par 'du byed pa'i stobs rgyun myi gcod cing mngon par 'du myi byed pa
2b3(mdo): shes pa'i rgyas/ lo zhugs pa sha stag go// thams cad kyang sems can gcig gi bya ba la/ bskal pa mtha' yas khar pyod pa la kun tu 'dzin par byin gyis rlom pa la mkhas la zha stag go// 
2b4(mdo): thams cad kye ba chud par chos kyi 'khor lo skor bar byin gyidas rlob cing gdul bya'i khams 'gro ba thams cad 'dzun pa la mkhas pa sha stag go// thams cad kyang 'das pa dang
2b5(mdo): ma 'jas pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rnam par dag pa'i gnas sa 'jug pa rlung spyod pa'i stobs kyi khyad par dang / smon skye thogs par
2b6(mdo): la gas go// thams cad kyang kun bya bzang po'i smon pa'i smon lam gyi khyad par gyi bsam pa mun tshogs pa ga cig go// bcos sun kyang sangs rgyas 'byub sa thams cad kyi bad du 'gro 'di skus
2b7(mdo): phrul mkhas pa shA stag go// thams cad kyang de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi chos kyi tshul kun tu 'dzin pa la mkhas pag sdug go// thams cad kyang sangs rgyas thams cad kyi rigs rgyun gyi
2b8(mdo): dpar byed pa zhe snyag go/ cad kyi sangs rgyas myed pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams su sangs rgyas 'byung ba kun tu ston par byed pa sha stag go// thams cang+ga k+Sha bkun nas/ nyon mongs
7a1(mdo): kyi 'jig rten dung su spyo pa byed pa sha stag go// thams cad kyang byed sase sus dpa' sems cad kyi las kyi snying rkyen gcod pa byed pa shasus so// thams
7a2(mdo): kyang chos kyi dbyings sgrib pa myed pa zhug la she lu ga zho/ thams cad kyang nam mkha'i khams lhan tshad myed pa'i chos dang ldan pa sha stag so// thams cad kyang chos kyi dbyings la 'jug pa sa
7a3(mdo): par smin y-i la/ mos pa sha stag go// thams cad kyang rgyus kun nas bslang ba ji lta ba bzhin du 'bras yul mos pan sdug go// thams cad kyang rgya'i 'a
7a4(mdo): 'byung ba y-i seM chos thams cad mnyam nyid du shes pa dang ldan pa sha stag go// thams cad kyang myig yor dang / gzugs brnyan ltar ston pa'i chos mnyam pa nyid dam
7a5(mdo): ldan pa ka s+t+wa~MhU~M g+ho// thams cad kyang chos thams cad kyi sgra dbyangs kyi rnam par rig pa phrag cha dang mtshungs pa dang ldan pan su'o// thams can kyang rna ze mo tha dad pa dang / ting nge 'dzin du
7a6(mdo): bsam gyis kyi khyal pA la gnas pa ga sug go// thams cad kyang dpa' bar 'gro ba'i ting nge 'dzin kyis rnam par chen bzha lug go// mas cad kyang seMngs rgyas kyi sku mtha' yas lnga'i
7a7(mdo): mchog yongs su grub pa sgrub pa'i gzungs la gnas pa sha stag go// thams cad kyang skams kyi nyon gtsigs 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kun tu mun pa yo du shu lhag s+ho/ 
7b1(mdo): tsam tu 'pha shes/ kha cig gis ni de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku dpag tshad tsam du 'phags par shes so// kha cig gis ni de bzhin gshegs pa brI dpaka tsad gnyis tsam du 'phags par shes pa
7b2(mdo): kha cig gis ni de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku dpan tshad bcu tsam du shes so// 'khor 'di nyid kyi nang nas kha cig gis ni bzhin gshegs pa'i sku dpag tshad stong du shes so// kha cig gis ni de bzhin
7b3(mdo): gshegs pa spu dpag tshad stong phrag bcu dang / nyi shu dang / sum bcu dang / bzhi bcu dang / lnga bcu dang zhes so// kha cin gos dpag dzar 'bum dang / kha cig gi ts+tsha mod bzhi
7b4(mdo): gshegs pa'i sku dpag tshad 'bum phrag bcu dang / shu dang / sum bcu dang / bzhi brgya dang / lnga bcu par shes ba khyod bzhin gshegs pa'i sku dpag chad bam+b+ha
7b5(mdo): nang nas kha cig gis ni de bzhin gshegs pa gse gyi kha dog tu mthong ngo // khaM cig gis ni nor bu rin po che byed du rgya'i kha dog tu/ kha cig gis ni nor bu rin po che chen po man da rnyil gyi rgya
7b6(mdo): cig cig gis ni nor bu rin po che mthon ka' chen po'i kha dog tu/ kha cig gis ni nor bu rin rje skad 'od gi kha dog tu khaT+wA~Mg gis ni nor bu rin po che par bya ral gyi kha dog du khacig gis ni nor bu'i nas
7b7(mdo): tshe dpya byin phyogs pa'ir don tu/ tshig gis ni nor bu rin po che rdo rje snang ba'i kha dog tu/ kha cig gron nor bu rin po che rnams cad snang ba'i kha dog tu/ cig gi tshan nor lha rin po che nyi zla snang ba'i
14a1(mdo): gos dri rdor bu rin po rgya mu 'dang gi kha dog tu/ kha cig gis ni de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku nor bu rin po chen+de gyi khadog tu shes so// b+hU tsig dim rI nor bu chen po che dbang
14a2(mdo): kyis ni nor bu rin po me 'od thangartsa cad bsgrus pa'i kha dog du/ kha cig gis ni nor bu rin po chergyal po ser ge ral ba can gyi kha dog tu ni nor bu rin po che se
14a3(mdo): mtshan gyi rtse mo 'i kha dog tu/ kha cig gis ni nor bu rin po che rgya mtsho'i gnas rnam par dag pa rin po che bkod pa/ kun nas 'od zer snang ba'i kha reg du ne so// 'jam dpal 'byor
14a4(mdo): nang nas/ kha cig gis ni de bzhin gshegs pa yid bzhin byi nor bu rin po che'i kha dog tu shes so// 'jam dpal kha dog dang / myod lam dang / dbyibasu gror rang gang zho nang
14a5(mdo): rnams 'atul por 'gyur ba/ 'jam dpal de bzhin gshegs ga' don dang / gyod lam dang / dbying pa de dang de kho nar se mas can rnams kyis mthong ngo // 
14a6(mdo): de bzhi gshegs pa'i bstan pa la 'dun cong 'dus bur 'byur ba'i khyod bad / sa de bzhin tshun nas pa bzhugs par mams can rnams kyi shes / 'dzas das gral gyi bar byonapa
14a7(mdo): 'din rte gyi bams dpag tu myed grangs byed/ thams kyis phyi byer/ mtshungs babyed gzhas du byed chad byed/ brjod du byed pa'i yang brjod du byed pa bya rgyum na bu dang / rkye sbyin
14b1(mdo): ma 'dres pa'i chos dang ldan pa'i phyir ro// 'jam dpal dper na sems can gyi las tha ma dang / 'bring dang / rab kyi rnam par smin pa'i dbang gis sems can rnams kyi 'du byed tha ma dang
14b2(mdo): 'bring dang / rab rnams 'byung yang 'du byed rnams ni mye tog rnam par myi tog ste/ 'on kyang 'du byed de dag lhun gyis grub cing rnam par myi rtog pa tha ma dang / 'bring dang / rab rnams
14b3(mdo): kyi bya ba dag la 'jug go// 'jam dpal de bzhin du de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas kyang sems can rnams kyi las kyi rnam par sbyin pa tha ma dang / 
14b4(mdo): 'bring dang / rab kyi dbang gis de bzhin gshegs pa thamadang / 'bring dang / rab tu sems can rnams kyis mthong yang 'jam dpal de bzhin gshegs pas ni myi tog rnam par
14b5(mdo): myi tog ste/ 'on kyang de bzhin gshegs pa ro'i mdzad bya de sta bu/ de spun gyis grub par 'byung ngo // 'jam dpa dper na nor bu rin po che byed du r+ya rigs mang ki ras pa dad pa nyid
14b6(mdo): kyi dbang gis ma dog tha dad pa nyid su 'gyur ro// 'jam dpal gal te nor bu rin po me bye ru r+ya ras ser po'i steng du bzhag na ni/ nor bu rin po che/ bye ru r+ya kha dog ser por 'gyur gal te/ ras dmar po'i snying / 
14b7(mdo): su bzhag ra ni/ nor bu rin po me bye du rtsal nog namar por 'gyur/ gal te ras sngon po'i steng du bzhag na ni/ nor bu rin po che bye du r+ya kha dog sngon por 'gyur te/ de ltar kha dog ci dang rtsi 'dra ba'i steng du bzhag pa de dang
14b8(mdo): de nyid chu dos bye ba'i kyar yang / 'jam dpal nor bu rin po che bye dUr+ya ni myi rtog rnam par myi rtog ste/ 'on kyang lhun gis grub cing rnam par myi rtog par de'i bya ba de lta bu de 'byung ngo // 'jam dpal de bzhi
16a1(mdo): hU~M de bzhin gshegs pa yang sems can tha 'ad pa nyid kyi dbang gis kha dog tha dad pa nyid du 'gyur te/ 'jam dpal gal te sems can rnams de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku gser gi kha dog tu mthong bas
16a2(mdo): la bar shA ni nan/ de dag gi sa de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku gser gi kha dog tu mthong ngo // gal te sems can nams nom thurin po che bye dU r+ya'i kha dog la bus rtul bar bya ba yin na ni/ de dag gis
16a3(mdo): byad de bzhin grashegs pa'i grwa nonar bu rin po kyi tsu t+ya'i khadog tu mamang // gas te sems can rnams su tig gi kha dog ga zhus gdus par bya bzhin nan/ de dag gis kyang de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku su
16a4(mdo): gi kha dog rgyu mthor ngo ro// gal te sems can rnams nor bu 'in po che man da rnyis kyi 'dog wA bu/ gdul bar bya ba yin na ni/ de dag gis kyang de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku nor bu rin po che man
16a5(mdo): nan+tas kyi kha dog tu mthang ngo // 'jas dpal gas te sems can rnam sa na bu rin po mamatshan ga chen po'i ma dog sa lus na/ dus 'am bya ba yin na ni/ de dag gis kyang de bzhin gshegs

16b1(mdo): bskal pa brjod du myed pa'i yang brjod du myed pa dag tu byin gyis rlob pa'i phyir tshe la dbang pa dang / ting nge 'dzin dpag tu myed grangs myed pa dag la nges par sems pa'i ye shes la 'jug pa'i/ 
16b2(mdo): phyir sems la dbang ba dang / 'jig rten gi khams thams cad bkod pa dang / rgyan du mas brgyan pa'i byin gyi brlabs kun tu ston pa'i phyir yo byad la dbang ba dang / 'jig rtend kyi
16b3(mdo): thams cad du skye ba kun tu ston pa'i phyir skye ba la dbang ba dang / dus ji lta ba bzhin du las kyi rnam par sbyin pa'i byin gyis brlabs pa kun tu bston pa'i phyir las la dpas dang / 'jig rten gyi
16b4(mdo): khams thams cad sangs rgyas kyis gang bar byin gyis rlo pa kun tu ston pa'i phyir mos pa la dbang pa dang / dus kA/ dang gang gi tshe/ byang chub mngon par rdzogs pam 'tshang rgya bar

16b6(mdo): grwa 'tshang rgya ba'i phyir smon lam la dbang ba dang / sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad du rdzu 'phrul dang / rnam par 'phrul ba kun tu ston pa'i phyir/ rdzu 'phrul la dbabya dang / mtha' dang dpung myed pa'i chos

31a1(mdo): 'jig rten gyi khams rnams 'jug par byed kyang / sems can kang la yang gnod pa dang / sgrib pa myed de sngon ji lta bar phyis kyang de bzhin no// bskal dpag tu myed grangs myed

32a1(mdo): gnyen gyis yongs su zin pa'i byang chub sems dpa' ni chos kyi dbyings lA yu khrel pa yang yin la/ sems can gyi khams la spyod yul par yang snang ngo // sangs rgyas kyi spyod yul

279a8(mdo): ma mchis la mnyen zhi snyan par smra ba dang / sA la yang ma mchis la byang chub kyi sems kyang myi 'dom pa dang / don dam pa spyod yul la yang lags la/ kun rdzob kyi srab pa'i rjes su yang 'jug ste/
